</div>
			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Primetime Emmy Award for Outstanding Comedy Series</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table class="infobox vevent" style="width:22em">
<tr>
<th colspan="2" class="summary" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;background-color: #eedd82;"><a href="/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Award" title="Primetime Emmy Award">Primetime Emmy Award</a> for Outstanding Comedy Series</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row" style="width: 33%;">Awarded for</th>
<td>Outstanding Comedy Series</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row" style="width: 33%;">Country</th>
<td class="location"><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row" style="width: 33%;">Presented by</th>
<td class="attendee"><a href="/wiki/Academy_of_Television_Arts_%26_Sciences" title="Academy of Television Arts &amp; Sciences">Academy of Television Arts &amp; Sciences</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row" style="width: 33%;">First awarded</th>
<td>1952</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row" style="width: 33%;">Currently held by</th>
<td><i><a href="/wiki/Veep" title="Veep">Veep</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/69th_Primetime_Emmy_Awards" title="69th Primetime Emmy Awards">2017</a>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row" style="width: 33%;">Website</th>
<td><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://emmys.com">emmys<wbr />.com</a></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>The <b><a href="/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Award" title="Primetime Emmy Award">Primetime Emmy Award</a> for Outstanding Comedy Series</b> is an annual award given to the best television comedy series of the year. From 1960 to 1964, this category was combined with the Comedy Specials (one time programs) category so that both type of programs competed for the same award during those years.</p>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/The_Flintstones" title="The Flintstones">The Flintstones</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Family_Guy" title="Family Guy">Family Guy</a></i> are the only animated series to be nominated for the award. Outside the <a href="/wiki/Big_Three_television_networks" title="Big Three television networks">Big Three networks (ABC, CBS and NBC)</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fox_Broadcasting_Company" title="Fox Broadcasting Company">Fox</a> has won this award twice, with <i><a href="/wiki/Ally_McBeal" title="Ally McBeal">Ally McBeal</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Arrested_Development_(TV_series)" title="Arrested Development (TV series)">Arrested Development</a></i> and <a href="/wiki/Cable_television" title="Cable television">cable network</a> <a href="/wiki/HBO" title="HBO">HBO</a> has won this award four times, one with <i><a href="/wiki/Sex_and_the_City" title="Sex and the City">Sex and the City</a></i> and three times with <i><a href="/wiki/Veep" title="Veep">Veep</a></i>.</p>
<p></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1960s">1960s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Primetime_Emmy_Award_for_Outstanding_Comedy_Series&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 1960s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="wikitable" style="width:100%">
<tr bgcolor="#BEBEBE">
<th width="5%">Year</th>
<th width="25%">Program</th>
<th width="65%">Producers</th>
<th width="5%">Network</th>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Total_awards_by_network">Total awards by network</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Primetime_Emmy_Award_for_Outstanding_Comedy_Series&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Total awards by network">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li>NBC – 26</li>
<li>CBS – 22</li>
<li>ABC – 11</li>
<li>HBO – 4</li>
<li>FOX – 2</li>
</ul>
